. 
. * also output the raw associations between deposits and traffic changes usin
> g stateXyear FEs 
. * only check the raw and logged deposits (after winsorization) this time
. foreach y of varlist depsumbr_w logdepsumbr_w {
  2.         foreach var of varlist delta_* {
  3.                 if "`var'" == "delta_devices_store" {
  4.                         reghdfe `y' `var', absorb(state_year_fe id_store)
>  
  5.                         outreg2 using "$tabdir/`y'_traffic_prediction_mod
> el_styr.xls", ///

> title("`y'") ///
>                         bracket bdec(4) sdec(4) replace ///
>                         addtext(Branch FE, Yes, StateXYear FE, Yes)     
  6.                 }
  7.                 else {
  8.                         reghdfe `y' `var', absorb(state_year_fe id_store)
>  
  9.                         outreg2 using "$tabdir/`y'_traffic_prediction_mod
> el_styr.xls", /// 
>                         title ("Annual Traffic Change on Branch Deposits") c
> title("`y'") ///
>                         bracket bdec(4) sdec(4) append ///
>                         addtext(Branch FE, Yes, StateXYear FE, Yes)
 10.                 }
 11.         }
 12.         * add clustering by state
.         foreach var of varlist delta_* {
 13.                 if "`var'" == "delta_devices_store" {
 14.                         reghdfe `y' `var', absorb(state_year_fe id_store)
>  vce(cl stnumb)
 15.                         outreg2 using "$tabdir/`y'_traffic_prediction_mod
> el_clst.xls", /// 
>                         title ("Annual Traffic Change on Branch Deposits") c
> title("`y'") ///
>                         bracket bdec(4) sdec(4) replace ///
>                         addtext(Branch FE, Yes, StateXYear FE, Yes, Note: st
> andard errors clustering at state level)    
 16.                 }
 17.                 else {
 18.                         reghdfe `y' `var', absorb(state_year_fe id_store)
>  vce(cl stnumb)
 19.                         outreg2 using "$tabdir/`y'_traffic_prediction_mod
> el_styr_clst.xls", /// 
>                         title ("Annual Traffic Change on Branch Deposits") c
> title("`y'") ///
>                         bracket bdec(4) sdec(4) append ///
>                         addtext(Branch FE, Yes, StateXYear FE, Yes, Note: st
> andard errors clustering at state level)
 20.                 }
 21.         }
 22.         * add clustering by county
.         foreach var of varlist delta_* {
